 ham apana vatan yaad aa rahaa tha
 (* change) We did not want to live in shame
 main yaqub ko kahati thi ki mujhe mahim ke machuaarine yaad aati hai
 i did not mention this incident because you have sympathy with Yakub
 dhamaake ke cese ko har din cover karne vaale patrkaar bhi kehete hai ki yaqub kaa maananaa tha ki is dhamaake main tiger memon hi kasuurvaar he
 Yakub, an intern in Pakistan, told Tiger Memon that i am going to Gandhi's country
 jawaab main tiger memon ne tha ki gandhi mat bano, aatmasamarpan mat karo
 Now all these things have not been confirmed concretely
 kaha yah jaataa he ki khufia agency or yaqub memon ke bich kuch deal hui jise yaqub ne bakhubi nibhaayaa
 Could the deal never come on record, so it could not help in the case
 na hi kabhi yaqub ne bataaya
 But it is true that Jacob handed himself to the law but also brought seven other members of his family to India
 yaqub ko laga ki badale main uske saath narmi barti jaaegi
 There is also a story that Yakub's lawyer at Kathmandu Airport prevented him from surrendering
 radiff kii shila bhatta ne jab vakil se pushti ke liye phone kiya to phone kaat diya
 Did not get an answer
 tippaniyan Senior Mumbai Police officer Rakesh Maria's investigation into the Mumbai bombings is no less than a saga for journalists covering the case
 maaria or mumbai police ne shandaar kaam kiya tha
 The case of Yakub's execution is currently at the point that preparations are being made for hanging on 30 July, twice the Supreme Court has rejected Yakub's petition, the President has done it and another time on Monday, the three judges of the Supreme Court Will hear on this

 com has published an unpublished article written by former intelligence officer late b Raman
 jise lekar dilli kii media main kaaphi charchaa he
 rediff
 com ne is lekh ko raman sahab ke bhai kii ijazat se chapa he
 Raman Saheb had told Sheela that he was saddened by the execution because it should have been taken care of that he helped the investigating agency and brought the rest of his family members to India
 raman us vakt ro kii pakistan desk ke mukhiya the
 He called Sheela Bhatt and said that India is doing a lot wrong
 ve is baat se aahat the ki unke adhikariyon ne mumbai court main jhooth bolaa he
 Yakub helped India, so it should be defended
 raman ne apni baat ko saarvajanik karne se manaa kiya tha kyonki ve nahin chaahate the ki duusare batch jaaen
 He said that the arrival of Yakub from Pakistan to India is a historic success of the Indian intelligence agency
 rajoana or bhullar kii faansee ke maamle main akali dal ke netaa khulkar virodh karte hai, (*change) akali dal kii saathi bijepi faansee kaa samarthan karti he lekin akali dal ko deshadrohi nahin kahati
 While hanging Afzal Guru, the Supreme Court has said a place in its judgment that hanging is necessary to satisfy the collective consciousness of the society
 ab hamen yaa aapako sochna chahie ki ye samuhik chetana kaise banati he
 If there is a collective consciousness about Afzal Guru and Yakub Memon then how does it diverge about the killers of Rajoana Bhullar or Rajiv Gandhi
 jo bhi he aisi tathakthith samuhik chetana hakeekat to he hi
 Remember, even during the Nirbhaya incident, a certain kind of fierce collective consciousness was daring to hang the killers of Nirbhaya
 baavjood uske balaatkaar kii sazaa ko sakht banane ke liye jute divangat justise verma ne apni report main faansee kii sazaa shaamil karne se inkaar kar diya us vakt raisina or puure desh kii samuhik chetana saream faansee dene kii bhi baat karti thi
 a few years later, in Delhi itself, a girl named Meenakshi is publicly killed with knives
 samuhik chetana nadaarad ho jaati he
 Justice Verma was right
 samuhik chetana ke bharose kanoon nahin chal saktaa
 i give another example of how collective consciousness can be formed
 hamaare aaj ke mehmaan or mashhoor vakil ujjwal nikam ne jaipur main kaha ki kasaab ke paksh main ban rahi hawa kaa rukh badalane ke liye unhone jhooth bolaa ki kasaab ne matan biryani kii maang kii
 This statement left the collective consciousness silent but many people were shocked
 pitiai ke anusaar nikam ne yah bhi bataaya ki biryani kii baat bataate hi media main panel discshan hone lage
 Kasab was a terrorist and even hanged, but when this false fact became part of the election sloganeering, then people of special religion in the name of Biryani started being targeted that a government was feeding Biryani to the terrorist in the wake of their vote
 isse hota yah he ki jo log faansee kii sazaa kaa hi virodh karte hai wo akele pad jate hai
 At the time of Afzal Guru's execution, when those who were being hanged were being called traitors, the prominent political thinker Pratap Bhanu Mehta wrote in the Indian Express that there were disagreements with the court's decision
 (*change) aise sawaal karnaa deshadroh nahin he balki loktantr majboot hi hota he
 (* change) Pratap Bhanu Mehta says that the Indian state has shown its weakness
 is baar saansad asadaduddin ovaisi ne mazahab se jodakar apane tareeke kii samuhik chetana gadhane kaa prayaas kiya he
 Because of which it has become really difficult to talk about the protest against the death penalty
 aisa lagata he ki kisi aatankwaadi ko mazahab ke naam par bachaaya ja rahaa he jabaki sawaal he ek bade cese ke zariye faansee kaa virodh
 Those opposing the execution have also opposed the hanging of Rajoana and Bhullar
 This is the talk of Yakub Memon whose death sentence is being commuted to life imprisonment
 1993 ke mumbai bam dhamaakon main tada adaalat ne yaqub memon ko faansee kii sazaa di he
 Even though 22 years have passed on the calendar, it was yesterday for Mumbai in which 257 people died and 700 people were injured
 yaqub memon mumbai dhamaake main faansee kii sazaa paane vaala 13waan shaks he
 rediff
 com par yaqub memon ke bare main shila bhatta ne ek saaf suthri or acchhee story likhi he
 Sheila was told by the lawyers associated with the case that she was sure of the punishment but was a little surprised that it would be hanged
 unka sawaal he ki yaqub kaa cese kya reerest aaf di rer he
 Tiger Memon and his family fled to Pakistan two days before the blast
 mumbai siriyal dhamaakon kaa mukhya aaropee tiger or daaud aaj bhi faraar hai lekin karachi main kuch din nazarband rahane ke baad yaqub memon bharat aane kaa faisla karata he
 Sheila Bhatt has written that her wife Rahin said that we came because we were under house arrest in Karachi
 hamen pasand nahin aayaa
 We were missing our country
 (*change) ham shame se nahin jeena chaahate the
 i used to tell Yakub that i miss Mahim's fishermen
 maine yah prasang isliye nahin bataaya ki aapako yaqub se sahanubhuti ho
 Journalists who cover the blast case every day also say that Yakub believed that Tiger Memon was the only culprit in this blast
 pakistan main nazarband yaqub ne tiger memon se kaha ki main gandhi ke desh ja rahaa hum
 In response, Tiger Memon said, "don't be Gandhi, don't surrender
" ab in sab baton kii tatthatmak pushti nahin hui he
 It is said that there was some deal between the intelligence agency and Yakub Memon, which Yakub did well
 kya deal hui kabhi ricard par nahin aa saki isliye usase mukademe main koi madad nahin mil saki
 Nor did Jacob ever tell
 lekin yah sahi he ki yaqub ne khud ko kanoon ke hawaale kiya balki apane parivaar ke anya saat sadasyon ko bhi bharat le aayaa
 Jacob felt that he would be softened in return
 ek kahani yah bhi he ki kathmandu airport par yaqub ke vakil ne use aatmasamarpan karne se roka tha
 Sheila Bhatt of Rediff disconnected the phone when she called for confirmation from the lawyer
 jawaab nahin mila
 The comments mumbai police ke varisht adhikari rakesh maaria ne mumbai bam dhamaake kii jo padtaal kii wo bhi is cese ko cover karne vaale patrakaron ke liye kisi gaatha se kam nahin he
 Maria and Mumbai Police did a fantastic job
 yaqub kii faansee kaa maamla philhal is mode par he ki 30 july ko faansee kii taiyaari ho rahi he, do baar supreme court ne yaqub kii yachika riject kii he, raashtrapati ne kii he or ek or baar somvaar ko supreme court kii teen jajon kii bench is par sunwaayee karegi

 com has printed this article with the permission of Raman Saheb's brother
 raman sahab ne shila ko bataaya tha ki ve faansee kii sazaa se dukhi hai kyonki is baat kaa khyaal rakhaa janaa chahie tha ki usne jaanch agency kii madad kii or apane parivaar ke baaki sadasyon ko bharat laayaa
 Raman was the head of Raw's Pakistan desk at the time
 unhone shila bhatta se phone kar kaha ki bharat bahut galat kar rahaa he
 He was hurt that his officers lied in Mumbai court
 yaqub ne bharat kii madad kii isliye uskaa bachaav kiya janaa chahie
 Raman refused to make his point public because he did not want others to survive
 unka kahana tha ki yaqub kaa pakistan se bharat le aana bhartiya khufia agency kii aitihaasik kamyaabi he
 According to PTI, Nikam also told that the panel discussion started in the media as soon as Biryani was told
 kasaab to aatankwaadi hi rahaa or faansee bhi hui lekin jab yah jhootha tathy chunavi narebaazi kaa hissaa bana to biryani ke naam se khaas mazahab ke logon ko nishaanaa banaaya jane laga ki ek sarkaar unke vot ke chakkar main aatankwaadi ko biryani khilaa rahi he
 It happens that those who oppose the execution of the sentence fall alone
 afzal guru kii faansee ke vakt jab faansee par sawaal karne waalon ko deshadrohi bataaya ja rahaa tha tab pramukh rajithik chintak pratap bhanu mehta ne indian express main likhaa ki adaalat ke faisle se asahmatiyaan hoti rahati hai
 (* change) Asking such questions is not treason but democracy is strong
 (*change) pratap bhanu mehta kehete hai ki bhartiya rajya ne apni kamazori hi pradarshit kii he
 This time MP Asaduddin Owaisi has tried to create a collective consciousness of his ways by connecting with religion
 jiske kaaran faansee kii sazaa ke virodh par baat karnaa vaaki mushkil ho gaya he
 It seems that a terrorist is being saved in the name of religion, whereas the question is to oppose the execution through a big case
 faansee kaa virodh karne waalon ne rajoana or bhullar kii faansee kaa bhi virodh kiya he yahi he yaqub memon jisaki faansee kii sazaa ko aaajeevan karawas main badalane kii baat ho rahi he
 Yakub Memon is hanged by the TADA court in the 1993 Mumbai blasts
 calendar par bhale hi 22 saal guzar gaye hon magar mumbai ke liye kal kii baat he jisamen 257 logon kii maut ho gai thi or 700 log ghayal ho gaye the
 Yakub Memon is the 13th person to be hanged in the Mumbai blast
 rediff
 com Sheila Bhatt has written a neat and good story about Yakub Memon
 shila ko is cese se jude vakeelon ne bataaya ki unhen sazaa kaa yakeen to tha magar faansee hogi is par thodaa chakit he
 His question is whether the case of Jacob is the rarest of the rare
 tiger memon or uskaa parivaar dhamaake se do din pehle pakistan bhaag gaya tha
 Tiger and Dawood, the main accused in the Mumbai serial blasts, are still absconding but after a few days of detention in Karachi, Yakub Memon decides to come to India
 shila bhatta ne likhaa he ki uski patni rahin ne kaha tha ki ham isliye aae kyonki ham karachi main nazarband the
 We did not like it
 ham apana vatan yaad aa rahaa tha
 (* change) We did not want to live in shame
 main yaqub ko kahati thi ki mujhe mahim ke machuaarine yaad aati hai
 i did not mention this incident because you have sympathy with Yakub
 dhamaake ke cese ko har din cover karne vaale patrkaar bhi kehete hai ki yaqub kaa maananaa tha ki is dhamaake main tiger memon hi kasuurvaar he
 Yakub, an intern in Pakistan, told Tiger Memon that i am going to Gandhi's country
 jawaab main tiger memon ne tha ki gandhi mat bano, aatmasamarpan mat karo
 Now all these things have not been confirmed concretely
 kaha yah jaataa he ki khufia agency or yaqub memon ke bich kuch deal hui jise yaqub ne bakhubi nibhaayaa
 Could the deal never come on record, so it could not help in the case
 na hi kabhi yaqub ne bataaya
 But it is true that Jacob handed himself to the law but also brought seven other members of his family to India
 yaqub ko laga ki badale main uske saath narmi barti jaaegi
 There is also a story that Yakub's lawyer at Kathmandu Airport prevented him from surrendering
 radiff kii shila bhatta ne jab vakil se pushti ke liye phone kiya to phone kaat diya

 tippaniyan Senior Mumbai Police officer Rakesh Maria's investigation into the Mumbai bombings is no less than a saga for journalists covering the case
 maaria or mumbai police ne shandaar kaam kiya tha

 rediff
 com ne is lekh ko raman sahab ke bhai kii ijazat se chapa he
 Raman Saheb had told Sheela that he was saddened by the execution because it should have been taken care of that he helped the investigating agency and brought the rest of his family members to India
 raman us vakt ro kii pakistan desk ke mukhiya the
 He called Sheela Bhatt and said that India is doing a lot wrong
 ve is baat se aahat the ki unke adhikariyon ne mumbai court main jhooth bolaa he
 Yakub helped India, so it should be defended
 raman ne apni baat ko saarvajanik karne se manaa kiya tha kyonki ve nahin chaahate the ki duusare batch jaaen
 He said that the arrival of Yakub from Pakistan to India is a historic success of the Indian intelligence agency
 isse hota yah he ki jo log faansee kii sazaa kaa hi virodh karte hai wo akele pad jate hai
 At the time of Afzal Guru's execution, when those who were being hanged were being called traitors, the prominent political thinker Pratap Bhanu Mehta wrote in the Indian Express that there were disagreements with the court's decision
 (*change) aise sawaal karnaa deshadroh nahin he balki loktantr majboot hi hota he
 (* change) Pratap Bhanu Mehta says that the Indian state has shown its weakness
 is baar saansad asadaduddin ovaisi ne mazahab se jodakar apane tareeke kii samuhik chetana gadhane kaa prayaas kiya he
 Because of which it has become really difficult to talk about the protest against the death penalty
 aisa lagata he ki kisi aatankwaadi ko mazahab ke naam par bachaaya ja rahaa he jabaki sawaal he ek bade cese ke zariye faansee kaa virodh
 Those opposing the execution have also opposed the hanging of Rajoana and Bhullar
 This is the talk of Yakub Memon whose death sentence is being commuted to life imprisonment
 1993 ke mumbai bam dhamaakon main tada adaalat ne yaqub memon ko faansee kii sazaa di he

 unka sawaal he ki yaqub kaa cese kya reerest aaf di rer he
 Tiger Memon and his family fled to Pakistan two days before the blast
 mumbai siriyal dhamaakon kaa mukhya aaropee tiger or daaud aaj bhi faraar hai lekin karachi main kuch din nazarband rahane ke baad yaqub memon bharat aane kaa faisla karata he

 hamen pasand nahin aayaa

 maine yah prasang isliye nahin bataaya ki aapako yaqub se sahanubhuti ho

" ab in sab baton kii tatthatmak pushti nahin hui he
